\documentclass[9pt]{article}

    \usepackage[breakable]{tcolorbox}
    \usepackage{parskip} % Stop auto-indenting (to mimic markdown behaviour)
    

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % Keep aspect ratio if custom image width or height is specified
    \setkeys{Gin}{keepaspectratio}
    % Maintain compatibility with old templates. Remove in nbconvert 6.0
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionFormat{nocaption}{}
    \captionsetup{format=nocaption,aboveskip=0pt,belowskip=0pt}

    \usepackage{float}
    \floatplacement{figure}{H} % forces figures to be placed at the correct location
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro

    \usepackage{iftex}
    \ifPDFTeX
        \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
        \IfFileExists{alphabeta.sty}{
              \usepackage{alphabeta}
          }{
              \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs}
              \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc}
          }
    \else
        \usepackage{fontspec}
        \usepackage{unicode-math}
    \fi

    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics
                         % to support a larger range
    \makeatletter % fix for old versions of grffile with XeLaTeX
    \@ifpackagelater{grffile}{2019/11/01}
    {
      % Do nothing on new versions
    }
    {
      \def\Gread@@xetex#1{%
        \IfFileExists{"\Gin@base".bb}%
        {\Gread@eps{\Gin@base.bb}}%
        {\Gread@@xetex@aux#1}%
      }
    }
    \makeatother
    \usepackage[Export]{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size
    \adjustboxset{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}

    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    % The default LaTeX title has an obnoxious amount of whitespace. By default,
    % titling removes some of it. It also provides customization options.
    \usepackage{titling}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage{array}     % table support for pandoc >= 2.11.3
    \usepackage{calc}      % table minipage width calculation for pandoc >= 2.11.1
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines
    \usepackage{soul}      % strikethrough (\st) support for pandoc >= 3.0.0
    \usepackage{mathrsfs}
    

    
    % Colors for the hyperref package
    \definecolor{urlcolor}{rgb}{0,.145,.698}
    \definecolor{linkcolor}{rgb}{.71,0.21,0.01}
    \definecolor{citecolor}{rgb}{.12,.54,.11}

    % ANSI colors
    \definecolor{ansi-black}{HTML}{3E424D}
    \definecolor{ansi-black-intense}{HTML}{282C36}
    \definecolor{ansi-red}{HTML}{E75C58}
    \definecolor{ansi-red-intense}{HTML}{B22B31}
    \definecolor{ansi-green}{HTML}{00A250}
    \definecolor{ansi-green-intense}{HTML}{007427}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow}{HTML}{DDB62B}
    \definecolor{ansi-yellow-intense}{HTML}{B27D12}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue}{HTML}{208FFB}
    \definecolor{ansi-blue-intense}{HTML}{0065CA}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta}{HTML}{D160C4}
    \definecolor{ansi-magenta-intense}{HTML}{A03196}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan}{HTML}{60C6C8}
    \definecolor{ansi-cyan-intense}{HTML}{258F8F}
    \definecolor{ansi-white}{HTML}{C5C1B4}
    \definecolor{ansi-white-intense}{HTML}{A1A6B2}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-fg}{HTML}{FFFFFF}
    \definecolor{ansi-default-inverse-bg}{HTML}{000000}

    % common color for the border for error outputs.
    \definecolor{outerrorbackground}{HTML}{FFDFDF}

    % commands and environments needed by pandoc snippets
    % extracted from the output of `pandoc -s`
    \providecommand{\tightlist}{%
      \setlength{\itemsep}{0pt}\setlength{\parskip}{0pt}}
    \DefineVerbatimEnvironment{Highlighting}{Verbatim}{commandchars=\\\{\}}
    % Add ',fontsize=\small' for more characters per line
    \newenvironment{Shaded}{}{}
    \newcommand{\KeywordTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\DataTypeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.56,0.13,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\DecValTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BaseNTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\FloatTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.63,0.44}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\StringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OtherTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AlertTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\FunctionTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.02,0.16,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\RegionMarkerTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ErrorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{1.00,0.00,0.00}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\NormalTok}[1]{{#1}}

    % Additional commands for more recent versions of Pandoc
    \newcommand{\ConstantTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.53,0.00,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialCharTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\VerbatimStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.25,0.44,0.63}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\SpecialStringTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.40,0.53}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ImportTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\DocumentationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.73,0.13,0.13}{\textit{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\AnnotationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\CommentVarTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\VariableTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.10,0.09,0.49}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\ControlFlowTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.00,0.44,0.13}{\textbf{{#1}}}}
    \newcommand{\OperatorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.40,0.40,0.40}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\BuiltInTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\ExtensionTok}[1]{{#1}}
    \newcommand{\PreprocessorTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.74,0.48,0.00}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\AttributeTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.49,0.56,0.16}{{#1}}}
    \newcommand{\InformationTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \newcommand{\WarningTok}[1]{\textcolor[rgb]{0.38,0.63,0.69}{\textbf{\textit{{#1}}}}}
    \makeatletter
    \newsavebox\pandoc@box
    \newcommand*\pandocbounded[1]{%
      \sbox\pandoc@box{#1}%
      % scaling factors for width and height
      \Gscale@div\@tempa\textheight{\dimexpr\ht\pandoc@box+\dp\pandoc@box\relax}%
      \Gscale@div\@tempb\linewidth{\wd\pandoc@box}%
      % select the smaller of both
      \ifdim\@tempb\p@<\@tempa\p@
        \let\@tempa\@tempb
      \fi
      % scaling accordingly (\@tempa < 1)
      \ifdim\@tempa\p@<\p@
        \scalebox{\@tempa}{\usebox\pandoc@box}%
      % scaling not needed, use as it is
      \else
        \usebox{\pandoc@box}%
      \fi
    }
    \makeatother

    % Define a nice break command that doesn't care if a line doesn't already
    % exist.
    \def\br{\hspace*{\fill} \\* }
    % Math Jax compatibility definitions
    \def\gt{>}
    \def\lt{<}
    \let\Oldtex\TeX
    \let\Oldlatex\LaTeX
    \renewcommand{\TeX}{\textrm{\Oldtex}}
    \renewcommand{\LaTeX}{\textrm{\Oldlatex}}
    % Document parameters
    % Document title
    \title{Appendix}
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
% Pygments definitions
\makeatletter
\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

\def\PYZbs{\char`\\}
\def\PYZus{\char`\_}
\def\PYZob{\char`\{}
\def\PYZcb{\char`\}}
\def\PYZca{\char`\^}
\def\PYZam{\char`\&}
\def\PYZlt{\char`\<}
\def\PYZgt{\char`\>}
\def\PYZsh{\char`\#}
\def\PYZpc{\char`\%}
\def\PYZdl{\char`\$}

    % For linebreaks inside Verbatim environment from package fancyvrb.
    \makeatletter
        \newbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox
        \newbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox
        \newcommand*\Wrappedvisiblespace {\textcolor{red}{\textvisiblespace}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol {\textcolor{red}{\llap{\tiny$\m@th\hookrightarrow$}}}
        \newcommand*\Wrappedcontinuationindent {3ex }
        \newcommand*\Wrappedafterbreak {\kern\Wrappedcontinuationindent\copy\Wrappedcontinuationbox}
        % Take advantage of the already applied Pygments mark-up to insert
        % potential linebreaks for TeX processing.
        %        {, <, #, %, $, ' and ": go to next line.
        %        _, }, ^, &, >, - and ~: stay at end of broken line.
        % Use of \textquotesingle for straight quote.
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatspecials {%
            \def\PYGZus{\discretionary{\char`\_}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\_}}%
            \def\PYGZob{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\{}{\char`\{}}%
            \def\PYGZcb{\discretionary{\char`\}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\}}}%
            \def\PYGZca{\discretionary{\char`\^}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\^}}%
            \def\PYGZam{\discretionary{\char`\&}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\&}}%
            \def\PYGZlt{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\<}{\char`\<}}%
            \def\PYGZgt{\discretionary{\char`\>}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\>}}%
            \def\PYGZsh{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\#}{\char`\#}}%
            \def\PYGZpc{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\%}{\char`\%}}%
            \def\PYGZdl{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\$}{\char`\$}}%
            \def\PYGZhy{\discretionary{\char`\-}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\-}}%
            \def\PYGZsq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\textquotesingle}{\textquotesingle}}%
            \def\PYGZdq{\discretionary{}{\Wrappedafterbreak\char`\"}{\char`\"}}%
            \def\PYGZti{\discretionary{\char`\~}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\char`\~}}%
        }
        % Some characters . , ; ? ! / are not pygmentized.
        % This macro makes them "active" and they will insert potential linebreaks
        \newcommand*\Wrappedbreaksatpunct {%
            \lccode`\~`\.\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\.}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\.}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\,\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\,}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\,}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\;\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\;}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\;}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\:\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\:}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\:}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\?\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\?}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\?}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\!\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\!}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\!}}}%
            \lccode`\~`\/\lowercase{\def~}{\discretionary{\hbox{\char`\/}}{\Wrappedafterbreak}{\hbox{\char`\/}}}%
            \catcode`\.\active
            \catcode`\,\active
            \catcode`\;\active
            \catcode`\:\active
            \catcode`\?\active
            \catcode`\!\active
            \catcode`\/\active
            \lccode`\~`\~
        }
    \makeatother

    \let\OriginalVerbatim=\Verbatim
    \makeatletter
    \renewcommand{\Verbatim}[1][1]{%
        %\parskip\z@skip
        \sbox\Wrappedcontinuationbox {\Wrappedcontinuationsymbol}%
        \sbox\Wrappedvisiblespacebox {\FV@SetupFont\Wrappedvisiblespace}%
        \def\FancyVerbFormatLine ##1{\hsize\linewidth
            \vtop{\raggedright\hyphenpenalty\z@\exhyphenpenalty\z@
                \doublehyphendemerits\z@\finalhyphendemerits\z@
                \strut ##1\strut}%
        }%
        % If the linebreak is at a space, the latter will be displayed as visible
        % space at end of first line, and a continuation symbol starts next line.
        % Stretch/shrink are however usually zero for typewriter font.
        \def\FV@Space {%
            \nobreak\hskip\z@ plus\fontdimen3\font minus\fontdimen4\font
            \discretionary{\copy\Wrappedvisiblespacebox}{\Wrappedafterbreak}
            {\kern\fontdimen2\font}%
        }%

        % Allow breaks at special characters using \PYG... macros.
        \Wrappedbreaksatspecials
        % Breaks at punctuation characters . , ; ? ! and / need catcode=\active
        \OriginalVerbatim[#1,codes*=\Wrappedbreaksatpunct]%
    }
    \makeatother

    % Exact colors from NB
    \definecolor{incolor}{HTML}{303F9F}
    \definecolor{outcolor}{HTML}{D84315}
    \definecolor{cellborder}{HTML}{CFCFCF}
    \definecolor{cellbackground}{HTML}{F7F7F7}

    % prompt
    \makeatletter
    \newcommand{\boxspacing}{\kern\kvtcb@left@rule\kern\kvtcb@boxsep}
    \makeatother
    \newcommand{\prompt}[4]{
        {\ttfamily\llap{{\color{#2}[#3]:\hspace{3pt}#4}}\vspace{-\baselineskip}}
    }
    

    
    % Prevent overflowing lines due to hard-to-break entities
    \sloppy
    % Setup hyperref package
    \hypersetup{
      breaklinks=true,  % so long urls are correctly broken across lines
      colorlinks=true,
      urlcolor=urlcolor,
      linkcolor=linkcolor,

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Dataframe has no null values
columns: 33, rows: 649
    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{Observations} - There are 33 columns, including the target
variable G3. - There are 649 observed students - Numeric columns show
expected ranges and summary statistics. - There are no missing values,
making preprocessing simpler.

    \hypertarget{preprocessing-the-data}{%
\subsection{Preprocessing the Data}\label{preprocessing-the-data}}

    \hypertarget{binary-encoding}{%
\subsubsection{Binary Encoding}\label{binary-encoding}}

Binary categorical features (e.g., sex, schoolsup) are mapped to 0/1 for
modeling:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{36}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}  Convert Binary Nominal Features to Binary Numeric \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Define binary mappings}
\PY{n}{binary\PYZus{}mappings} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{school}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{GP}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{MS}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sex}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{M}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{F}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{address}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{U}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{R}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{famsize}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{GT3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{LE3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Pstatus}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{T}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{A}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{schoolsup}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{famsup}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{paid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{activities}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{nursery}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{higher}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{internet}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
    \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{romantic}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{yes}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{no}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Make a copy of the raw dataframe}
\PY{n}{df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}raw}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Apply mappings column by column and ensure integer type}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{mapping} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{binary\PYZus{}mappings}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{items}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{col} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{map}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{mapping}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Save the preprocessed dataset}
\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{to\PYZus{}csv}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{../data/student\PYZus{}preprocessed.csv}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{index}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Display the updated dataframe}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
None
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \textbf{Explanation} - Binary variables are converted for computation in
models like OLS and tree-based algorithms. - Four multi-category nominal
variables remain (dtype: object) and will be one-hot encoded later -
Data set is clean and ready for analysis

    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_15_0.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \textbf{Observations} - Most variables are approximately symmetric,
except absences (right-skewed). - Boxplots reveal outliers in absences
and some grades (G1, G2). - The target G3 is left-skewed, we will
address this later

\textbf{Interpretation} - Skewed variables may require transformations
in some models. - Outliers can affect OLS estimates; we'll consider
removing them.

    \hypertarget{numeric-relationships-with-g3}{%
\subsubsection{Numeric Relationships with
G3}\label{numeric-relationships-with-g3}}

Scatterplots with regression lines show linear associations:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{40}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Scatter Plots \PYZam{} Regression vs G3 for Numeric Variables \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Remove \PYZsq{}G3\PYZsq{} to avoid plotting vs itself}
\PY{n}{numeric\PYZus{}vars} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{var} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{numeric\PYZus{}vars} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{var} \PY{o}{!=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Determine grid size}
\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}vars} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{numeric\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cols} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}
\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{int}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{ceil}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}vars} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{fig}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axes} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subplots}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cols}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n\PYZus{}cols}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n\PYZus{}rows}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{axes} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{axes}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{flatten}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Loop through variables and plot scatter + regression vs G3}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{col} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{numeric\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Calculate correlation coefficient}
    \PY{n}{r} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{corr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{n}{sns}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{regplot}\PY{p}{(}
        \PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{scatter\PYZus{}kws}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{alpha}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.5}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{line\PYZus{}kws}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{color}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{red}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}title}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{G3 vs }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{col}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ (r = }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{r}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.2f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Remove any unused axes}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{j} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{fig}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{delaxes}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{axes}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\begin{itemize}

  G1 and G2 show the strongest correlation with G3
  (\(r \approx 0.83 \& 0.92\)).
\item
  Other variables like famrel show weak correlations.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{association-strength-for-categorical-variables}{%
\subsubsection{Association Strength for Categorical
Variables}\label{association-strength-for-categorical-variables}}

We compute Pearson correlations for binary and eta-squared for
multi-category features:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{43}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Association Strength for Categorical Variables \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Identify categorical variables}
\PY{n}{categorical\PYZus{}cols} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{results} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{col} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{:}  
    \PY{n}{unique\PYZus{}vals} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropna}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{unique}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Binary variable → use Pearson (point\PYZhy{}biserial)}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{unique\PYZus{}vals}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{n+nb}{set}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{unique\PYZus{}vals}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{issubset}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{corr}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pval} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pearsonr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Variable}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Type}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Binary}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Correlation}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{corr}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{pval}
        \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Multi\PYZhy{}category variable → use eta\PYZhy{}squared (from ANOVA)}
    \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{unique\PYZus{}vals}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{groups} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{val}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{dropna}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{val} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{unique\PYZus{}vals}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{f\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{pval} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{f\PYZus{}oneway}\PY{p}{(}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{ss\PYZus{}between} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{g}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{*} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{g}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{2} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{g} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{groups}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{ss\PYZus{}total} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{*}\PY{o}{*}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{eta\PYZus{}sq} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ss\PYZus{}between} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{ss\PYZus{}total} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{ss\PYZus{}total} \PY{o}{!=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nan}
        \PY{n}{results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Variable}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{col}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Type}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Multi\PYZhy{}Category}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Correlation}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{eta\PYZus{}sq}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{pval}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert to DataFrame and sort}
\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{results}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{results\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{results\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{by}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{|Correlation|}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ascending}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}

    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_33_0.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \textbf{Explanation:}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Shows the absolute correlation / eta-squared values across all
  variables.
\item
  Facilitates quick identification of the most influential features.
\end{itemize}

    \hypertarget{chi-square-tests-for-categorical-variables}{%
\subsubsection{Chi Square Tests for Categorical
Variables}\label{chi-square-tests-for-categorical-variables}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{46}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Chi\PYZhy{}square Tests for Categorical Variables \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{n}{alpha} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} significance threshold}

\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}results} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{j} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{i}\PY{o}{+}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{var1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{var2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{cat\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{j}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Contingency table}
        \PY{n}{table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{crosstab}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var2}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{chi2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dof}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{expected} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}contingency}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{table}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Cramer\PYZsq{}s V effect size}
        \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
        \PY{n}{cramers\PYZus{}v} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{chi2} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{min\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0} \PY{k}{else} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nan}

        \PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Variable 1}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{var1}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Variable 2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{var2}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Chi2}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{chi2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{dof}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{dof}\PY{p}{,}
            \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cramer}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s V}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cramers\PYZus{}v}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reset\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Significant Chi\PYZhy{}square results (p \PYZlt{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{alpha}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{):}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{display}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{alpha}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Largest effect sizes (Cramer}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s V):}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{display}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{chi2\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cramer}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s V}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ascending}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{head}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{10}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \textbf{Interpretation}

Althought there are several significant tests to say there may be some
correlation between variables, the highest effect size (Cramer's V) is
0.413, which is only a moderate strength of association. We shouldn't
have to worry about strong associastions here.

    \hypertarget{inferential-statistics}{%
\subsection{Inferential Statistics}\label{inferential-statistics}}

    \hypertarget{t-tests-for-binary-categorical-variables-vs-g3}{%
\subsubsection{T-tests for Binary Categorical Variables vs
G3}\label{t-tests-for-binary-categorical-variables-vs-g3}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{47}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} T\PYZhy{}tests for Binary Categorical vs G3 \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{n}{alpha} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} significance threshold}

\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n}{target} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} target variable}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{var} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{bin\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{:}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} binary predictors}
    \PY{n}{group0} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{group1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{==} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{]}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Variance ratio}
    \PY{n}{var0} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ddof}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{var1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{ddof}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{ratio} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{max}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{var0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{var1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n+nb}{min}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{var0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{var1}\PY{p}{)}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Choose t\PYZhy{}test type}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{ratio} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mf}{1.5}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{t\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ttest\PYZus{}ind}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{group1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equal\PYZus{}var}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}type} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Welch}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s t\PYZhy{}test}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}
    \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{n}{t\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ttest\PYZus{}ind}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group0}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{group1}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{equal\PYZus{}var}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}type} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Student}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s t\PYZhy{}test}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Effect size (Cohen\PYZsq{}s d)}
    \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}diff} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{group1}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{group0}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{pooled\PYZus{}sd} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sqrt}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{var0} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{var1}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{cohens\PYZus{}d} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{mean\PYZus{}diff} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{pooled\PYZus{}sd}

    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Append results}
    \PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Binary Variable}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Target Variable}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Test Type}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{test\PYZus{}type}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{t\PYZhy{}statistic}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Variance Ratio}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{ratio}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Group0 Mean}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group0}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Group1 Mean}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{group1}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Cohen}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{s d}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{cohens\PYZus{}d}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Convert to DataFrame}
\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results\PYZus{}df}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reset\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Significant t\PYZhy{}test results (p \PYZlt{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{alpha}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{):}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{display}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{t\PYZus{}results\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{alpha}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Significant t-test results (p < 0.05):
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \textbf{Observations}

Students who attend GP school, have internet access, plan for higher
education, and live in urban areas tend to achieve significantly higher
final grades (G3). Conversely, those receiving school support, in
romantic relationships, or female students show slightly lower average
grades, though these effects are smaller in magnitude.

    \hypertarget{anova-tests-for-multi-level-categorical-variables-vs-g3}{%
\subsubsection{ANOVA Tests for Multi-level Categorical Variables vs
G3}\label{anova-tests-for-multi-level-categorical-variables-vs-g3}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{48}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} ANOVA for Multi\PYZhy{}level Categorical vs Continuous \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{n}{alpha} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.05}
\PY{n}{target} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}results} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{var} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{ord\PYZus{}vars}\PY{p}{:}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} ordinal/multi\PYZhy{}level categorical predictors}
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Skip variables with less than 2 levels}
    \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{nunique}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{:}
        \PY{k}{continue}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Fit ANOVA model}
    \PY{n}{model} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{ols}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{target}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ \PYZti{} C(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{var}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{n}{df}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{stats}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}lm}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{model}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{typ}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{n}{f\PYZus{}stat} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{var}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{F}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    \PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{var}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{PR(\PYZgt{}F)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}
    
    \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Eta\PYZhy{}squared: sum\PYZus{}sq\PYZus{}var / sum\PYZus{}sq\PYZus{}total}
    \PY{n}{eta\PYZus{}sq} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}table}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{C(}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{var}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{)}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{sum\PYZus{}sq}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}table}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{sum\PYZus{}sq}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
    
    \PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}results}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{\PYZob{}}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Categorical Variable}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{var}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Target Variable}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{target}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{F\PYZhy{}statistic}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{f\PYZus{}stat}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p\PYZus{}val}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{5}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
        \PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Eta\PYZhy{}squared}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{eta\PYZus{}sq}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{)}
    \PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}df} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pd}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{DataFrame}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}results}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sort\PYZus{}values}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reset\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Significant ANOVA results (p \PYZlt{} }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{alpha}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{):}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{display}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{anova\PYZus{}df}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{alpha}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Significant ANOVA results (p < 0.05):
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
   Categorical Variable Target Variable  F-statistic  p-value  Eta-squared
0                  Medu              G3       10.764  0.00000        0.063
1                  Fedu              G3        8.223  0.00000        0.049
2             studytime              G3       15.876  0.00000        0.069
3              failures              G3       51.386  0.00000        0.193
4                  Dalc              G3        8.193  0.00000        0.048
5                 goout              G3        6.986  0.00002        0.042
6                  Walc              G3        5.535  0.00022        0.033
7              freetime              G3        4.489  0.00139        0.027
8                famrel              G3        3.678  0.00568        0.022
9            traveltime              G3        3.659  0.01232        0.017
10               health              G3        2.440  0.04574        0.015
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \textbf{Observations}

Students' final grades (G3) vary significantly across several
multi-level factors: higher parental education, more study time, and
fewer past failures are strongly linked to better performance, while
frequent alcohol use, more going out, and longer travel times are
associated with lower grades. Overall, failures and studytime show the
largest effect sizes (\(η² \approx 0.19\) and \(0.07\)).

    \hypertarget{checking-model-assumptions}{%

Assumptions}\label{checking-model-assumptions}}

    \textbf{Interpretation}

G3 is clearly right-skewed, we will need to see if removing the outliers
makes the distribution more normal.

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    \textbf{Observations}

Removing the outliers helped shape G3 to be more normally distributed.
G3 shifted from heavily left skewed to slightly right skewed. Even
though G3 with outliers removed still doesn't pass the Shapiro-Wilk
significance test, the QQ plot for G3 gives enough reason to suggest we
can assume a normally distributed target variable

    \hypertarget{multicollinearity-of-categorical-predictors}{%

Predictors}\label{multicollinearity-of-categorical-predictors}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{51}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Check Multicollinearity (VIF) with One\PYZhy{}hot Encoded Multi\PYZhy{}category Predictors \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} X = predictors only (after one\PYZhy{}hot encoding)}

\PY{n}{X} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{sm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{add\PYZus{}constant}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{p}{)}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} add intercept}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Compute VIF}

\PY{n}{vif\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Variable}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns}
\PY{n}{vif\PYZus{}data}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{VIF}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{variance\PYZus{}inflation\PYZus{}factor}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{values}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Sort descending for readability}

9  Mjob\_services    2.113154
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \textbf{Interpretation}

The variance inflation factor (VIF) analysis indicates that
multicollinearity among the predictor variables is generally low. All
predictors exhibit VIF values below 5, suggesting that redundancy
between variables is minimal and should not adversely affect the
stability of the regression estimates. The exceptionally high VIF for
the intercept (const) is expected and does not indicate
multicollinearity among the predictors.

    \hypertarget{heteroscedasticity}{%
\subsubsection{Heteroscedasticity}\label{heteroscedasticity}}

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{53}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}  \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Test for Heteroscedasticity (Breusch\PYZhy{}Pagan) \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Residuals and predictors from preliminary OLS model}
\PY{n}{lm} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prelim\PYZus{}model}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} your OLS model}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Run Breusch\PYZhy{}Pagan test}
\PY{n}{bp\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{het\PYZus{}breuschpagan}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{resid}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{lm}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{model}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{exog}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{bp\PYZus{}labels} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{LM Statistic}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{LM p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{F\PYZhy{}Statistic}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{F p\PYZhy{}value}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{Breusch\PYZhy{}Pagan Test for Heteroscedasticity:}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{label}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{value} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{zip}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{bp\PYZus{}labels}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{bp\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{f}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{label}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{: }\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{value}\PY{l+s+si}{:}\PY{l+s+s2}{.4f}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
\end{tcolorbox}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Breusch-Pagan Test for Heteroscedasticity:
LM Statistic: 67.3687
LM p-value: 0.0058
F-Statistic: 1.7168
F p-value: 0.0043
    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{Observation}

The test indicates significant heteroscedasticity, as evidenced by
p-values near zero, leading to rejection of the null hypothesis.
Consequently, OLS estimates may have inefficient standard errors; it is
recommended to use robust standard errors and consider alternative
modeling approaches that are less sensitive to heteroscedasticity, such
as tree-based methods like Random Forest or Gradient Boosting.

    \hypertarget{modeling}{%
\subsection{Modeling}\label{modeling}}

    \hypertarget{feature-engineering}{%
\subsubsection{Feature Engineering}\label{feature-engineering}}

We will test an OLS model with few interaction terms to see if we should
include them in our final model:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{54}{\boxspacing}
\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{} Feature Engineering \PYZam{} Interaction Terms \PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}\PYZhy{}}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}encoded}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{drop}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{columns}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}no\PYZus{}outliers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G3}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 1. Performance improvement (abs difference between G1 and G2)}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G\PYZus{}perf\PYZus{}improve}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{abs}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}no\PYZus{}outliers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}no\PYZus{}outliers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 2. Average past performance (G1 + G2)/2}
\PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G\PYZus{}avg}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{df\PYZus{}no\PYZus{}outliers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G1}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{df\PYZus{}no\PYZus{}outliers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{G2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 3. Interaction term (studytime * failures)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{studytime}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{failures}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns}\PY{p}{:}
    \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{studytime\PYZus{}failures}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{studytime}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{failures}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}

\PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 4. Interaction term (absences * studytime)}
\PY{k}{if} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{absences}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns} \PY{o+ow}{and} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{studytime}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{X\PYZus{}test\PYZus{}fe}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{columns}\PY{p}{:}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
Baseline OLS Test R2: 0.8949719417225516
Baseline OLS Test RMSE: 0.8717123735429568
FE OLS Test R2: 0.8940081828334319
FE OLS Test RMSE: 0.8757027456172547
    \end{Verbatim}

    \textbf{Observation}

The test set results show no improvement after adding the
feature-engineered and interaction terms. R² and RMSE are largely
unchanged, indicating these features do not add meaningful predictive
value.

    \hypertarget{comparing-models}{%
\subsubsection{Comparing Models}\label{comparing-models}}

We will use all predictors to choose the best model between OLS, Lasso,
Ridge, Random Forest, and Gradient Boosting:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
               Model  Train\_RMSE  Test\_RMSE  Train\_R2   Test\_R2
0                OLS    0.800243   0.871712  0.908518  0.894972
1              Lasso    0.848957   0.890324  0.897041  0.890439
2              Ridge    0.802309   0.877693  0.908045  0.893526
3      Random Forest    0.334208   0.861520  0.984044  0.897414
4  Gradient Boosting    0.425179   0.868352  0.974175  0.895780
    \end{Verbatim}

    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_65_1.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_65_2.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \textbf{Explanation}

We selected the Random Forest as the best-performing model because it
achieved the lowest test set RMSE. The violin plots show that its
residuals are tightly clustered around zero, with a narrow, symmetric
shape and the shortest range among models, indicating accurate
predictions with low variance.

A test R² of 0.897 indicates that approximately 89.7\% of the variance
in the target variable is explained by the model on unseen data. This
suggests a very strong predictive performance, meaning the model
captures most of the systematic patterns in the data, with only about
10\% of the variance left unexplained.

A test RMSE of 0.861 indicates that, on average, the model's predictions
deviate from the true values by about 0.86 units. Combined with a high
R², this shows that the model predicts the target variable accurately,
with relatively small errors.

Forest)}\label{interpreting-the-best-model-random-forest}}

    \textbf{Interpretation}

The model's residuals are approximately normal and homoscedastic. The
strongest predictors of G3 are G2, G1, absences, and age.

    \hypertarget{comparing-models-again-without-g1-and-g2-as-predictors}{%
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Comparing Models (again) \texttt{Without}
`G1' and `G2' as
Predictors}{Comparing Models (again) Without `G1' and `G2' as Predictors}}\label{comparing-models-again-without-g1-and-g2-as-predictors}}

We will remove `G1' and `G2' and choose the best model between OLS,
Lasso, Ridge, Random Forest, and Gradient Boosting:

    \begin{tcolorbox}[breakable, size=fbox, boxrule=1pt, pad at break*=1mm,colback=cellbackground, colframe=cellborder]
\prompt{In}{incolor}{57}{\boxspacing}

\PY{n}{X} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{X}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{loc}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{y}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{]}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
               Model  Train\_RMSE  Test\_RMSE  Train\_R2   Test\_R2
0                OLS    2.076106   2.122731  0.384270  0.377200
1              Lasso    2.128481   2.161344  0.352812  0.354336
2              Ridge    2.087657   2.101231  0.377399  0.389752
3      Random Forest    0.815488   2.146161  0.904999  0.363375
4  Gradient Boosting    1.186433   2.231479  0.798916  0.311753
    \end{Verbatim}

    
    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_71_1.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \begin{center}
    \adjustimage{max size={0.9\linewidth}{0.9\paperheight}}{main_files/main_71_2.png}
    \end{center}
    { \hspace*{\fill} \\}
    
    \textbf{Explanation}

We selected Ridge regression as the best-performing model because it
achieved the lowest test set RMSE. The violin plots show that its
residuals are tightly clustered around zero, with short tails indicating
a small range of errors. Although the zero line runs through the center
of the Lasso residuals as well, Ridge was preferred due to its slightly
lower RMSE, reflected in the narrower distribution of residuals.

As expected, the predictive power of this model with G1 and G2 removed
is much lower (r2 = .39), although the purpose is to analyze how the
other feature importances will change without the G1 and G2 predictors.
We will do this next.

    \hypertarget{interpreting-best-model-again-without-g1-and-g2-as-predictors-ridge}{%

\texttt{Without} `G1' and `G2' as Predictors
(Ridge)}{Interpreting Best Model (again) Without `G1' and `G2' as Predictors (Ridge)}}\label{interpreting-best-model-again-without-g1-and-g2-as-predictors-ridge}}

    \textbf{Interpretation:}

The model's residuals are approximately normal and homoscedastic. The
strongest predictors in this model with G1 and G2 removed are now
failuers, higher (pursuit of higher education), absences, schoolsup
(level of academic support), and school.
